## Section 3: Data File Schemas

### vehicles.txt
- Stores: All vehicle details for renting, availability and pricing.
- Format (pipe-delimited):
  vehicle_id|make|model|vehicle_type|daily_rate|seats|transmission|fuel_type|status
- Fields:
  - vehicle_id: int
  - make: str
  - model: str
  - vehicle_type: str (Economy, Compact, Sedan, SUV, Luxury)
  - daily_rate: float
  - seats: int
  - transmission: str (Automatic, Manual)
  - fuel_type: str (Petrol, Diesel, Electric, Hybrid)
  - status: str (Available, Unavailable)
- Example lines:
  1|Toyota|Camry|Sedan|55.00|5|Automatic|Petrol|Available
  2|Honda|CR-V|SUV|75.00|7|Automatic|Petrol|Available
  3|BMW|X5|Luxury|150.00|5|Automatic|Diesel|Available


### customers.txt
- Stores: All customer personal and license info.
- Format:
  customer_id|name|email|phone|driver_license|license_expiry
- Fields:
  - customer_id: int
  - name: str
  - email: str
  - phone: str
  - driver_license: str
  - license_expiry: date (YYYY-MM-DD)
- Examples:
  1|Alice Johnson|alice@example.com|555-0101|D1234567|2026-06-15
  2|Bob Williams|bob@example.com|555-0102|D2345678|2027-03-20


### locations.txt
- Stores: Rental locations and availability
- Format:
  location_id|city|address|phone|hours|available_vehicles
- Fields:
  - location_id: int
  - city: str
  - address: str
  - phone: str
  - hours: str (24/7, 09:00-18:00, etc.)
  - available_vehicles: int
- Examples:
  1|New York|123 Main St, NYC|555-1000|24/7|12
  2|Los Angeles|456 Oak Ave, LA|555-2000|09:00-18:00|8


### rentals.txt
- Stores: Rental transactions with dates, locations, pricing, status
- Format:
  rental_id|vehicle_id|customer_id|pickup_date|dropoff_date|pickup_location|dropoff_location|total_price|status
- Fields:
  - rental_id: int
  - vehicle_id: int
  - customer_id: int
  - pickup_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)
  - dropoff_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)
  - pickup_location: str (city or specific location name)
  - dropoff_location: str
  - total_price: float
  - status: str (Completed, Active, Cancelled)
- Examples:
  1|1|1|2025-02-01|2025-02-05|New York|Los Angeles|275.00|Completed
  2|2|2|2025-02-10|2025-02-12|Los Angeles|New York|150.00|Active


### insurance.txt
- Stores: Insurance plan options for rentals
- Format:
  insurance_id|plan_name|description|daily_cost|coverage_limit|deductible
- Fields:
  - insurance_id: int
  - plan_name: str
  - description: str
  - daily_cost: float
  - coverage_limit: str|int (e.g., 50000 or "Unlimited")
  - deductible: int or float
- Examples:
  1|Basic Coverage|Liability only, min coverage|5.00|50000|1000
  2|Standard Coverage|Collision and theft protection|12.00|250000|500
  3|Premium Coverage|Full comprehensive protection|18.00|Unlimited|0


### reservations.txt
- Stores: Reservation details tied to rentals with insurance and special requests
- Format:
  reservation_id|rental_id|vehicle_id|customer_id|status|insurance_id|special_requests
- Fields:
  - reservation_id: int
  - rental_id: int
  - vehicle_id: int
  - customer_id: int
  - status: str (Confirmed, Active, Cancelled)
  - insurance_id: int
  - special_requests: str (free text)
- Examples:
  1|1|1|1|Confirmed|2|Driver assistance requested
  2|2|2|2|Active|1|GPS and child seat needed


---

END OF DESIGN SPECIFICATIONS

    # Filtering vehicles by availability and attributes     if location_filter:         # Assuming availability is checked based on rental locations and status         rentals = load_rentals() datetime.strptime(r['return_date'], '%Y-%m-%d')                 if r['status'] == 'Active' and (pickup <= ed and dropoff >= sd):                     unavailable_ids.add(r['vehicle_id']) 'POST']) def booking():     vehicles = load_vehicles()     locations = load_locations()      if request.method == 'POST':         vehicle_id = int(request.form.get('vehicle_id')) # CarRental Web Application Design Specifications

---

## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification (Backend)

| Route Path                 | Function Name           | HTTP Method(s) | Template File              | Context Variables                                                                                  |
|----------------------------|-------------------------|----------------|----------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| /                          | root_redirect           | GET            | N/A (redirect to /dashboard) | None                                                                                             |
| /dashboard                 | dashboard               | GET            | dashboard.html              | featured_vehicles: list[dict], promotions: list[dict]                                           |
| /search                   | vehicle_search          | GET            | search.html                 | vehicles: list[dict], locations: list[dict], vehicle_types: list[str], filters: dict[str,str]   |
| /vehicle/<int:vehicle_id> | vehicle_details         | GET            | vehicle_details.html        | vehicle: dict, reviews: list[dict]                                                              |
| /booking                  | booking                 | GET, POST      | booking.html                | pickup_locations: list[dict], dropoff_locations: list[dict], calculated_price: float or None     |
| /insurance                | insurance_options       | GET, POST      | insurance.html              | insurance_plans: list[dict], selected_insurance: dict or None                                   |
| /rental-history           | rental_history          | GET            | rental_history.html         | rentals: list[dict], status_filter: str                                                          |
| /reservations             | reservations_management | GET, POST      | reservations.html           | reservations: list[dict]                                                                         |
| /special-requests         | special_requests        | GET, POST      | special_requests.html       | reservations: list[dict], form_data: dict or None                                               |
| /locations                | locations_page          | GET            | locations.html              | locations: list[dict], hours_filter: str, search_query: str                                     |

### Route Details

- **/** (root_redirect): redirects to `/dashboard` to enforce dashboard as the start page.
- **/dashboard**: Displays main dashboard with featured vehicles and promotions.

  - featured_vehicles: List of vehicle dictionaries including vehicle_id, make, model, daily_rate, etc.
  - promotions: List of promotion dictionaries, each containing title, description.

- **/search**: Displays search page with filters and all vehicles matching filters.

  - vehicles: List of vehicle dictionaries with availability and details.
  - locations: List of location dictionaries for filtering.
  - vehicle_types: List[str] of vehicle type strings (`Economy`, `Compact`, `Sedan`, `SUV`, `Luxury`).
  - filters: Dict[str,str] current filter values for location, vehicle_type, date_range.

- **/vehicle/<int:vehicle_id>**: Shows detailed information about one vehicle.

  - vehicle: Dict with vehicle fields.
  - reviews: List of review dicts related to vehicle.

- **/booking**: Displays and processes booking form.

  - GET context: pickup_locations, dropoff_locations.
  - POST context: same + calculated_price (float) after price calculation.

- **/insurance**: Insurance options selection page.

  - insurance_plans: List of insurance dictionaries.
  - selected_insurance: Selected insurance dictionary or None.

- **/rental-history**: Displays rental history.

  - rentals: List of rental dictionaries.
  - status_filter: Current selected status filter (e.g., "All", "Active", etc.)

- **/reservations**: Manages reservations with possible actions POSTed.

  - reservations: List of reservation dictionaries.

- **/special-requests**: Add special requests to selected reservation.

  - reservations: List of current reservations.
  - form_data: Dict of submitted special requests or None.

- **/locations**: Displays locations with filters and search.

  - locations: List of location dictionaries.
  - hours_filter: Current hours filter value.
  - search_query: Current text search query string.


---

## Section 2: HTML Template Specifications (Frontend)

### 1. templates/dashboard.html
- Page Title: Car Rental Dashboard
- Element IDs:

  - search-vehicles-button (Button): Navigates to vehicle search page via url_for('vehicle_search').
  - my-reservations-button (Button): Navigates to reservations page via url_for('reservations_management').
  - promotions-section (Div): Displays current promotions and offers.
- Navigation:
  - search-vehicles-button: url_for('vehicle_search')
  - my-reservations-button: url_for('reservations_management')
- Context Variables:
  - featured_vehicles: list of dict with vehicle fields.
  - promotions: list of dict with promotion fields.

- Element IDs:

  - date-range-input (Input): Rental date range input
  - vehicles-grid (Div): Grid container for vehicle cards
  - view-details-button-{vehicle_id} (Button): Each vehicle's details button with dynamic id, where {vehicle_id} is vehicle's ID

---

## Section 3: Data File Schemas

### vehicles.txt
- Stores: All vehicle details for renting, availability and pricing.
- Format (pipe-delimited):
  vehicle_id|make|model|vehicle_type|daily_rate|seats|transmission|fuel_type|status
- Fields:
  - vehicle_id: int
  - make: str
  - model: str
  - vehicle_type: str (Economy, Compact, Sedan, SUV, Luxury)
  - daily_rate: float
  - seats: int
  - transmission: str (Automatic, Manual)
  - fuel_type: str (Petrol, Diesel, Electric, Hybrid)
  - status: str (Available, Unavailable)
- Example lines:
  1|Toyota|Camry|Sedan|55.00|5|Automatic|Petrol|Available
  2|Honda|CR-V|SUV|75.00|7|Automatic|Petrol|Available
  3|BMW|X5|Luxury|150.00|5|Automatic|Diesel|Available


### customers.txt
- Stores: All customer personal and license info.
- Format:
  customer_id|name|email|phone|driver_license|license_expiry
- Fields:
  - customer_id: int
  - name: str
  - email: str
  - phone: str
  - driver_license: str
  - license_expiry: date (YYYY-MM-DD)
- Examples:
  1|Alice Johnson|alice@example.com|555-0101|D1234567|2026-06-15
  2|Bob Williams|bob@example.com|555-0102|D2345678|2027-03-20


### locations.txt
- Stores: Rental locations and availability
- Format:
  location_id|city|address|phone|hours|available_vehicles
- Fields:
  - location_id: int
  - city: str
  - address: str
  - phone: str
  - hours: str (24/7, 09:00-18:00, etc.)
  - available_vehicles: int
- Examples:
  1|New York|123 Main St, NYC|555-1000|24/7|12
  2|Los Angeles|456 Oak Ave, LA|555-2000|09:00-18:00|8


### rentals.txt
- Stores: Rental transactions with dates, locations, pricing, status
- Format:
  rental_id|vehicle_id|customer_id|pickup_date|dropoff_date|pickup_location|dropoff_location|total_price|status
- Fields:
  - rental_id: int
  - vehicle_id: int
  - customer_id: int
  - pickup_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)
  - dropoff_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)
  - pickup_location: str (city or specific location name)
  - dropoff_location: str
  - total_price: float
  - status: str (Completed, Active, Cancelled)
- Examples:
  1|1|1|2025-02-01|2025-02-05|New York|Los Angeles|275.00|Completed
  2|2|2|2025-02-10|2025-02-12|Los Angeles|New York|150.00|Active


### insurance.txt
- Stores: Insurance plan options for rentals
- Format:
  insurance_id|plan_name|description|daily_cost|coverage_limit|deductible
- Fields:
  - insurance_id: int
  - plan_name: str
  - description: str
  - daily_cost: float
  - coverage_limit: str|int (e.g., 50000 or "Unlimited")
  - deductible: int or float
- Examples:
  1|Basic Coverage|Liability only, min coverage|5.00|50000|1000
  2|Standard Coverage|Collision and theft protection|12.00|250000|500
  3|Premium Coverage|Full comprehensive protection|18.00|Unlimited|0


### reservations.txt
- Stores: Reservation details tied to rentals with insurance and special requests
- Format:
  reservation_id|rental_id|vehicle_id|customer_id|status|insurance_id|special_requests
- Fields:
  - reservation_id: int
  - rental_id: int
  - vehicle_id: int
  - customer_id: int
  - status: str (Confirmed, Active, Cancelled)
  - insurance_id: int
  - special_requests: str (free text)
- Examples:
  1|1|1|1|Confirmed|2|Driver assistance requested
  2|2|2|2|Active|1|GPS and child seat needed


---

END OF DESIGN SPECIFICATIONS


=== app.py ===
from flask import Flask, render_template, request, redirect, url_for
import csv
from datetime import datetime

app = Flask(__name__)

# Data loading helper functions

def load_vehicles():
    vehicles = []
    with open('vehicles.txt', 'r') as f:
        reader = csv.DictReader(f, delimiter='|', fieldnames=['vehicle_id', 'make', 'model', 'vehicle_type', 'daily_rate', 'seats', 'transmission', 'fuel_type', 'status'])
        for row in reader:
            try:
                row['vehicle_id'] = int(row['vehicle_id'])
                row['daily_rate'] = float(row['daily_rate'])
                row['seats'] = int(row['seats'])
                vehicles.append(row)
            except Exception:
                continue
    return vehicles

def load_customers():
    customers = []
    with open('customers.txt', 'r') as f:
        reader = csv.DictReader(f, delimiter='|', fieldnames=['customer_id', 'name', 'email', 'phone', 'driver_license', 'license_expiry'])
        for row in reader:
            try:
                row['customer_id'] = int(row['customer_id'])
                customers.append(row)
            except Exception:
                continue
    return customers

def load_locations():
    locations = []
    with open('locations.txt', 'r') as f:
        reader = csv.DictReader(f, delimiter='|', fieldnames=['location_id', 'city', 'address', 'hours'])
        for row in reader:
            try:
                row['location_id'] = int(row['location_id'])
                locations.append(row)
            except Exception:
                continue
    return locations

def load_rentals():
    rentals = []
    with open('rentals.txt', 'r') as f:
        reader = csv.DictReader(f, delimiter='|', fieldnames=['rental_id', 'vehicle_id', 'customer_id', 'pickup_date', 'return_date', 'pickup_location', 'dropoff_location', 'status'])
        for row in reader:
            try:
                row['rental_id'] = int(row['rental_id'])
                row['vehicle_id'] = int(row['vehicle_id'])
                row['customer_id'] = int(row['customer_id'])
                # validate dates
                datetime.strptime(row['pickup_date'], '%Y-%m-%d')
                datetime.strptime(row['return_date'], '%Y-%m-%d')
                rentals.append(row)
            except Exception:
                continue
    return rentals

def load_insurance():
    plans = []
    with open('insurance.txt', 'r') as f:
        reader = csv.DictReader(f, delimiter='|', fieldnames=['insurance_id', 'name', 'description', 'daily_cost', 'coverage_limit', 'deductible'])
        for row in reader:
            try:
                row['insurance_id'] = int(row['insurance_id'])
                row['daily_cost'] = float(row['daily_cost'])
                row['coverage_limit'] = float(row['coverage_limit'])
                row['deductible'] = float(row['deductible'])
                plans.append(row)
            except Exception:
                continue
    return plans

def load_reservations():
    reservations = []
    with open('reservations.txt', 'r') as f:
        reader = csv.DictReader(f, delimiter='|', fieldnames=['reservation_id', 'vehicle_id', 'customer_id', 'rental_id', 'status', 'special_requests', 'insurance_id', 'assistance_needed'])
        for row in reader:
            try:
                row['reservation_id'] = int(row['reservation_id'])
                row['vehicle_id'] = int(row['vehicle_id'])
                row['customer_id'] = int(row['customer_id'])
                row['rental_id'] = int(row['rental_id'])
                if row['status'] not in ['Confirmed', 'Cancelled']:
                    row['status'] = 'Confirmed'
                reservations.append(row)
            except Exception:
                continue
    return reservations

# Home - Redirect to dashboard
@app.route('/')
def home():
    return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))

# Dashboard - shows featured vehicles and promotions
@app.route('/dashboard')
def dashboard():
    vehicles = load_vehicles()
    featured_vehicles = vehicles[:5]  # Example: first 5 as featured
    promotions = [
        {'id': 1, 'description': '10% off on all Sedans!'},
        {'id': 2, 'description': 'Free GPS with SUV rentals over 3 days.'}
    ]
    return render_template('dashboard.html', featured_vehicles=featured_vehicles, promotions=promotions)

# Vehicle Search Page
@app.route('/search', methods=['GET'])
def vehicle_search():
    vehicles = load_vehicles()
    locations = load_locations()
    vehicle_types = list(set(v['vehicle_type'] for v in vehicles))

    # Filter parameters
    location_filter = request.args.get('location', None)
    vehicle_type_filter = request.args.get('vehicle_type', None)
    start_date = request.args.get('start_date', None)
    end_date = request.args.get('end_date', None)

    filtered_vehicles = vehicles

    # Filtering vehicles by availability and attributes
    if location_filter:
        # Assuming availability is checked based on rental locations and status
        rentals = load_rentals()
        unavailable_vehicle_ids = set()
        for r in rentals:
            if r['pickup_location'] == location_filter and r['status'] == 'Active':
                # Assume vehicle unavailable during this rental period
                unavailable_vehicle_ids.add(r['vehicle_id'])
        filtered_vehicles = [v for v in filtered_vehicles if v['vehicle_id'] not in unavailable_vehicle_ids]

    if vehicle_type_filter:
        filtered_vehicles = [v for v in filtered_vehicles if v['vehicle_type'] == vehicle_type_filter]

    # Date range filtering: naive, assuming vehicles unavailable in date range if rental overlaps
    if start_date and end_date:
        try:
            sd = datetime.strptime(start_date, '%Y-%m-%d')
            ed = datetime.strptime(end_date, '%Y-%m-%d')
            rentals = load_rentals()
            unavailable_ids = set()
            for r in rentals:
                pickup = datetime.strptime(r['pickup_date'], '%Y-%m-%d')
                dropoff = datetime.strptime(r['return_date'], '%Y-%m-%d')
                if r['status'] == 'Active' and (pickup <= ed and dropoff >= sd):
                    unavailable_ids.add(r['vehicle_id'])
            filtered_vehicles = [v for v in filtered_vehicles if v['vehicle_id'] not in unavailable_ids]
        except Exception:
            pass

    return render_template('search.html', vehicles=filtered_vehicles, locations=locations, vehicle_types=vehicle_types)

# Vehicle Details Page
@app.route('/vehicle/<int:vehicle_id>')
def vehicle_details(vehicle_id):
    vehicles = load_vehicles()
    vehicle = next((v for v in vehicles if v['vehicle_id'] == vehicle_id), None)
    if not vehicle:
        return 'Vehicle not found', 404

    # Load reviews from a reviews.txt (not specified in data) mock empty list
    reviews = []

    return render_template('vehicle_details.html', vehicle=vehicle, reviews=reviews)

# Booking Page
@app.route('/booking', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def booking():
    vehicles = load_vehicles()
    locations = load_locations()

    if request.method == 'POST':
        vehicle_id = int(request.form.get('vehicle_id'))
        pickup_location = request.form.get('pickup_location')
        dropoff_location = request.form.get('dropoff_location')
        pickup_date = request.form.get('pickup_date')
        dropoff_date = request.form.get('dropoff_date')

        # Compute price
        vehicle = next((v for v in vehicles if v['vehicle_id'] == vehicle_id), None)
        if not vehicle:
            return 'Invalid vehicle', 400

        try:
            pd = datetime.strptime(pickup_date, '%Y-%m-%d')
            dd = datetime.strptime(dropoff_date, '%Y-%m-%d')
            days = (dd - pd).days + 1
        except Exception:
            days = 1

        calculated_price = days * vehicle['daily_rate']

        return render_template('booking.html', vehicles=vehicles, locations=locations, calculated_price=calculated_price, selected_vehicle=vehicle)
    else:
        return render_template('booking.html', vehicles=vehicles, locations=locations, calculated_price=None, selected_vehicle=None)

# Insurance Options Page
@app.route('/insurance', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def insurance_options():
    insurance_plans = load_insurance()
    selected_insurance = None

    if request.method == 'POST':
        insurance_id = request.form.get('insurance_id')
        if insurance_id:
            try:
                insurance_id = int(insurance_id)
                selected_insurance = next((i for i in insurance_plans if i['insurance_id'] == insurance_id), None)
            except Exception:
                selected_insurance = None

    return render_template('insurance.html', insurance_plans=insurance_plans, selected_insurance=selected_insurance)

# Locations Page
@app.route('/locations')
def locations_page():
    locations = load_locations()
    city_filter = request.args.get('city', None)
    if city_filter:
        locations = [l for l in locations if city_filter.lower() in l['city'].lower()]
    return render_template('locations.html', locations=locations, city_filter=city_filter)

[DEBUG] Review Content for FrontendDeveloper -> SystemArchitect:
  [design_spec.md] # CarRental Web Application Design Specifications  ---  ## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification (Backend)  | Route Path                 | Function Name           | HTTP Method(s) | Template File              | Context Variables                                                                                  | |----------------------------|-------------------------|----------------|----------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------| | /                          | root_redirect           | GET            | N/A (redirect to /dashboard) | None                                                                                             | | /dashboard                 | dashboard               | GET            | dashboard.html              | featured_vehicles: list[dict], promotions: list[dict]                                           | | /search                   | vehicle_search          | GET            | search.html                 | vehicles: list[dict], locations: list[dict], vehicle_types: list[str], filters: dict[str,str]   | | /vehicle/<int:vehicle_id> | vehicle_details         | GET            | vehicle_details.html        | vehicle: dict, reviews: list[dict]                                                              | | /booking                  | booking                 | GET, POST      | booking.html                | pickup_locations: list[dict], dropoff_locations: list[dict], calculated_price: float or None     | | /insurance                | insurance_options       | GET, POST      | insurance.html              | insurance_plans: list[dict], selected_insurance: dict or None                                   | | /rental-history           | rental_history          | GET            | rental_history.html         | rentals: list[dict], status_filter: str                                                          | | /reservations             | reservations_management | GET, POST      | reservations.html           | reservations: list[dict]                                                                         | | /special-requests         | special_requests        | GET, POST      | special_requests.html       | reservations: list[dict], form_data: dict or None                                               | | /locations                | locations_page          | GET            | locations.html              | locations: list[dict], hours_filter: str, search_query: str                                     |  ### Route Details  - **/** (root_redirect): redirects to `/dashboard` to enforce dashboard as the start page. - **/dashboard**: Displays main dashboard with featured vehicles and promotions.    - featured_vehicles: List of vehicle dictionaries including vehicle_id, make, model, daily_rate, etc.   - promotions: List of promotion dictionaries, each containing title, description.  - **/search**: Displays search page with filters and all vehicles matching filters.    - vehicles: List of vehicle dictionaries with availability and details.   - locations: List of location dictionaries for filtering.   - vehicle_types: List[str] of vehicle type strings (`Economy`, `Compact`, `Sedan`, `SUV`, `Luxury`).   - filters: Dict[str,str] current filter values for location, vehicle_type, date_range.  - **/vehicle/<int:vehicle_id>**: Shows detailed information about one vehicle.    - vehicle: Dict with vehicle fields.   - reviews: List of review dicts related to vehicle.  - **/booking**: Displays and processes booking form.    - GET context: pickup_locations, dropoff_locations.   - POST context: same + calculated_price (float) after price calculation.  - **/insurance**: Insurance options selection page.    - insurance_plans: List of insurance dictionaries.   - selected_insurance: Selected insurance dictionary or None.  - **/rental-history**: Displays rental history.    - rentals: List of rental dictionaries.   - status_filter: Current selected status filter (e.g., "All", "Active", etc.)  - **/reservations**: Manages reservations with possible actions POSTed.    - reservations: List of reservation dictionaries.  - **/special-requests**: Add special requests to selected reservation.    - reservations: List of current reservations.   - form_data: Dict of submitted special requests or None.  - **/locations**: Displays locations with filters and search.    - locations: List of location dictionaries.   - hours_filter: Current hours filter value.   - search_query: Current text search query string.   ---  ## Section 2: HTML Template Specifications (Frontend)  ### 1. templates/dashboard.html - Page Title: Car Rental Dashboard - Element IDs:   - dashboard-page (Div): Container for full dashboard page.   - featured-vehicles (Div): Display of featured vehicle recommendations.   - search-vehicles-button (Button): Navigates to vehicle search page via url_for('vehicle_search').   - my-reservations-button (Button): Navigates to reservations page via url_for('reservations_management').   - promotions-section (Div): Displays current promotions and offers. - Navigation:   - search-vehicles-button: url_for('vehicle_search')   - my-reservations-button: url_for('reservations_management') - Context Variables:   - featured_vehicles: list of dict with vehicle fields.   - promotions: list of dict with promotion fields.   ### 2. templates/search.html - Page Title: Search Vehicles - Element IDs:   - search-page (Div): Container   - location-filter (Dropdown): Filter by pickup location   - vehicle-type-filter (Dropdown): Filter by vehicle type   - date-range-input (Input): Rental date range input   - vehicles-grid (Div): Grid container for vehicle cards   - view-details-button-{vehicle_id} (Button): Each vehicle's details button with dynamic id, where {vehicle_id} is vehicle's ID - Navigation:   - view-details-button-{vehicle_id}: url_for('vehicle_details', vehicle_id=vehicle_id) - Context Variables:   - vehicles: list of dict   - locations: list of dict   - vehicle_types: list of str   - filters: dict with keys "location", "vehicle_type", "date_range"   ### 3. templates/vehicle_details.html - Page Title: Vehicle Details - Element IDs:   - vehicle-details-page (Div)   - vehicle-name (H1)   - vehicle-specs (Div)   - daily-rate (Div)   - book-now-button (Button): navigates to /booking page with preselected vehicle?   - vehicle-reviews (Div) - Navigation:   - book-now-button: url_for('booking') - Context Variables:   - vehicle: dict   - reviews: list of dict   ### 4. templates/booking.html - Page Title: Book Your Rental - Element IDs:   - booking-page (Div)   - pickup-location (Dropdown)   - dropoff-location (Dropdown)   - pickup-date (Input)   - dropoff-date (Input)   - calculate-price-button (Button): triggers price calculation   - total-price (Div): shows calculated price   - proceed-to-insurance-button (Button): navigates to insurance options - Navigation:   - proceed-to-insurance-button: url_for('insurance_options') - Context Variables:   - pickup_locations: list of dict   - dropoff_locations: list of dict   - calculated_price: float or None   ### 5. templates/insurance.html - Page Title: Select Insurance Coverage - Element IDs:   - insurance-page (Div)   - insurance-options (Div): container for insurance plans   - select-insurance-{insurance_id} (Radio): select insurance plan   - insurance-description (Div): shows selected insurance description   - insurance-price (Div): shows selected insurance price   - confirm-booking-button (Button) - Navigation:   - confirm-booking-button: submits insurance selection, possibly redirects - Context Variables:   - insurance_plans: list of dict   - selected_insurance: dict or None   ### 6. templates/rental_history.html - Page Title: Rental History - Element IDs:   - history-page (Div)   - rentals-table (Table): columns: ID, vehicle, dates, location, status   - view-rental-details-{rental_id} (Button): view details of rental   - status-filter (Dropdown)   - back-to-dashboard (Button): url_for('dashboard') - Navigation:   - back-to-dashboard: url_for('dashboard') - Context Variables:   - rentals: list of dict   - status_filter: str   ### 7. templates/reservations.html - Page Title: My Reservations - Element IDs:   - reservations-page (Div)   - reservations-list (Div): list all reservations   - modify-reservation-button-{reservation_id} (Button)   - cancel-reservation-button-{reservation_id} (Button)   - sort-by-date-button (Button)   - back-to-dashboard (Button): url_for('dashboard') - Navigation:   - back-to-dashboard: url_for('dashboard') - Context Variables:   - reservations: list of dict   ### 8. templates/special_requests.html - Page Title: Special Requests - Element IDs:   - requests-page (Div)   - select-reservation (Dropdown)   - driver-assistance-checkbox (Checkbox)   - gps-option-checkbox (Checkbox)   - child-seat-quantity (Input)   - special-notes (Textarea)   - submit-requests-button (Button) - Navigation:   - submit-requests-button: submits form data - Context Variables:   - reservations: list of dict   - form_data: dict or None   ### 9. templates/locations.html - Page Title: Pickup and Dropoff Locations - Element IDs:   - locations-page (Div)   - locations-list (Div)   - location-detail-button-{location_id} (Button)   - hours-filter (Dropdown)   - search-location-input (Input)   - back-to-dashboard (Button): url_for('dashboard') - Navigation:   - back-to-dashboard: url_for('dashboard') - Context Variables:   - locations: list of dict   - hours_filter: str   - search_query: str   ---  ## Section 3: Data File Schemas  ### vehicles.txt - Stores: All vehicle details for renting, availability and pricing. - Format (pipe-delimited):   vehicle_id|make|model|vehicle_type|daily_rate|seats|transmission|fuel_type|status - Fields:   - vehicle_id: int   - make: str   - model: str   - vehicle_type: str (Economy, Compact, Sedan, SUV, Luxury)   - daily_rate: float   - seats: int   - transmission: str (Automatic, Manual)   - fuel_type: str (Petrol, Diesel, Electric, Hybrid)   - status: str (Available, Unavailable) - Example lines:   1|Toyota|Camry|Sedan|55.00|5|Automatic|Petrol|Available   2|Honda|CR-V|SUV|75.00|7|Automatic|Petrol|Available   3|BMW|X5|Luxury|150.00|5|Automatic|Diesel|Available   ### customers.txt - Stores: All customer personal and license info. - Format:   customer_id|name|email|phone|driver_license|license_expiry - Fields:   - customer_id: int   - name: str   - email: str   - phone: str   - driver_license: str   - license_expiry: date (YYYY-MM-DD) - Examples:   1|Alice Johnson|alice@example.com|555-0101|D1234567|2026-06-15   2|Bob Williams|bob@example.com|555-0102|D2345678|2027-03-20   ### locations.txt - Stores: Rental locations and availability - Format:   location_id|city|address|phone|hours|available_vehicles - Fields:   - location_id: int   - city: str   - address: str   - phone: str   - hours: str (24/7, 09:00-18:00, etc.)   - available_vehicles: int - Examples:   1|New York|123 Main St, NYC|555-1000|24/7|12   2|Los Angeles|456 Oak Ave, LA|555-2000|09:00-18:00|8   ### rentals.txt - Stores: Rental transactions with dates, locations, pricing, status - Format:   rental_id|vehicle_id|customer_id|pickup_date|dropoff_date|pickup_location|dropoff_location|total_price|status - Fields:   - rental_id: int   - vehicle_id: int   - customer_id: int   - pickup_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)   - dropoff_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)   - pickup_location: str (city or specific location name)   - dropoff_location: str   - total_price: float   - status: str (Completed, Active, Cancelled) - Examples:   1|1|1|2025-02-01|2025-02-05|New York|Los Angeles|275.00|Completed   2|2|2|2025-02-10|2025-02-12|Los Angeles|New York|150.00|Active   ### insurance.txt - Stores: Insurance plan options for rentals - Format:   insurance_id|plan_name|description|daily_cost|coverage_limit|deductible - Fields:   - insurance_id: int   - plan_name: str   - description: str   - daily_cost: float   - coverage_limit: str|int (e.g., 50000 or "Unlimited")   - deductible: int or float - Examples:   1|Basic Coverage|Liability only, min coverage|5.00|50000|1000   2|Standard Coverage|Collision and theft protection|12.00|250000|500   3|Premium Coverage|Full comprehensive protection|18.00|Unlimited|0   ### reservations.txt - Stores: Reservation details tied to rentals with insurance and special requests - Format:   reservation_id|rental_id|vehicle_id|customer_id|status|insurance_id|special_requests - Fields:   - reservation_id: int   - rental_id: int   - vehicle_id: int   - customer_id: int   - status: str (Confirmed, Active, Cancelled)   - insurance_id: int   - special_requests: str (free text) - Examples:   1|1|1|1|Confirmed|2|Driver assistance requested   2|2|2|2|Active|1|GPS and child seat needed   ---  END OF DESIGN SPECIFICATIONS

# CarRental Web Application Design Specifications

---

## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification (Backend)

| Route Path                 | Function Name           | HTTP Method(s) | Template File              | Context Variables                                                                                  |
|----------------------------|-------------------------|----------------|----------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| /                          | root_redirect           | GET            | N/A (redirect to /dashboard) | None                                                                                             |
| /dashboard                 | dashboard               | GET            | dashboard.html              | featured_vehicles: list[dict], promotions: list[dict]                                           |
| /search                   | vehicle_search          | GET            | search.html                 | vehicles: list[dict], locations: list[dict], vehicle_types: list[str], filters: dict[str,str]   |
| /vehicle/<int:vehicle_id> | vehicle_details         | GET            | vehicle_details.html        | vehicle: dict, reviews: list[dict]                                                              |
| /booking                  | booking                 | GET, POST      | booking.html                | pickup_locations: list[dict], dropoff_locations: list[dict], calculated_price: float or None     |
| /insurance                | insurance_options       | GET, POST      | insurance.html              | insurance_plans: list[dict], selected_insurance: dict or None                                   |
| /rental-history           | rental_history          | GET            | rental_history.html         | rentals: list[dict], status_filter: str                                                          |
| /reservations             | reservations_management | GET, POST      | reservations.html           | reservations: list[dict]                                                                         |
| /special-requests         | special_requests        | GET, POST      | special_requests.html       | reservations: list[dict], form_data: dict or None                                               |
| /locations                | locations_page          | GET            | locations.html              | locations: list[dict], hours_filter: str, search_query: str                                     |

### Route Details

- **/** (root_redirect): redirects to `/dashboard` to enforce dashboard as the start page.
- **/dashboard**: Displays main dashboard with featured vehicles and promotions.

  - featured_vehicles: List of vehicle dictionaries including vehicle_id, make, model, daily_rate, etc.
  - promotions: List of promotion dictionaries, each containing title, description.

- **/search**: Displays search page with filters and all vehicles matching filters.

  - vehicles: List of vehicle dictionaries with availability and details.
  - locations: List of location dictionaries for filtering.
  - vehicle_types: List[str] of vehicle type strings (`Economy`, `Compact`, `Sedan`, `SUV`, `Luxury`).
  - filters: Dict[str,str] current filter values for location, vehicle_type, date_range.

- **/vehicle/<int:vehicle_id>**: Shows detailed information about one vehicle.

  - vehicle: Dict with vehicle fields.
  - reviews: List of review dicts related to vehicle.

- **/booking**: Displays and processes booking form.

  - GET context: pickup_locations, dropoff_locations.
  - POST context: same + calculated_price (float) after price calculation.

- **/insurance**: Insurance options selection page.

  - insurance_plans: List of insurance dictionaries.
  - selected_insurance: Selected insurance dictionary or None.

- **/rental-history**: Displays rental history.

  - rentals: List of rental dictionaries.
  - status_filter: Current selected status filter (e.g., "All", "Active", etc.)

- **/reservations**: Manages reservations with possible actions POSTed.

  - reservations: List of reservation dictionaries.

- **/special-requests**: Add special requests to selected reservation.

  - reservations: List of current reservations.
  - form_data: Dict of submitted special requests or None.

- **/locations**: Displays locations with filters and search.

  - locations: List of location dictionaries.
  - hours_filter: Current hours filter value.
  - search_query: Current text search query string.


---

## Section 2: HTML Template Specifications (Frontend)

### 1. templates/dashboard.html
- Page Title: Car Rental Dashboard
- Element IDs:
  - dashboard-page (Div): Container for full dashboard page.
  - featured-vehicles (Div): Display of featured vehicle recommendations.
  - search-vehicles-button (Button): Navigates to vehicle search page via url_for('vehicle_search').
  - my-reservations-button (Button): Navigates to reservations page via url_for('reservations_management').
  - promotions-section (Div): Displays current promotions and offers.
- Navigation:
  - search-vehicles-button: url_for('vehicle_search')
  - my-reservations-button: url_for('reservations_management')
- Context Variables:
  - featured_vehicles: list of dict with vehicle fields.
  - promotions: list of dict with promotion fields.


### 2. templates/search.html
- Page Title: Search Vehicles
- Element IDs:
  - search-page (Div): Container
  - location-filter (Dropdown): Filter by pickup location
  - vehicle-type-filter (Dropdown): Filter by vehicle type
  - date-range-input (Input): Rental date range input
  - vehicles-grid (Div): Grid container for vehicle cards
  - view-details-button-{vehicle_id} (Button): Each vehicle's details button with dynamic id, where {vehicle_id} is vehicle's ID
- Navigation:
  - view-details-button-{vehicle_id}: url_for('vehicle_details', vehicle_id=vehicle_id)
- Context Variables:
  - vehicles: list of dict
  - locations: list of dict
  - vehicle_types: list of str
  - filters: dict with keys "location", "vehicle_type", "date_range"


### 3. templates/vehicle_details.html
- Page Title: Vehicle Details
- Element IDs:
  - vehicle-details-page (Div)
  - vehicle-name (H1)
  - vehicle-specs (Div)
  - daily-rate (Div)
  - book-now-button (Button): navigates to /booking page with preselected vehicle?
  - vehicle-reviews (Div)
- Navigation:
  - book-now-button: url_for('booking')
- Context Variables:
  - vehicle: dict
  - reviews: list of dict


### 4. templates/booking.html
- Page Title: Book Your Rental
- Element IDs:
  - booking-page (Div)
  - pickup-location (Dropdown)
  - dropoff-location (Dropdown)
  - pickup-date (Input)
  - dropoff-date (Input)
  - calculate-price-button (Button): triggers price calculation
  - total-price (Div): shows calculated price
  - proceed-to-insurance-button (Button): navigates to insurance options
- Navigation:
  - proceed-to-insurance-button: url_for('insurance_options')
- Context Variables:
  - pickup_locations: list of dict
  - dropoff_locations: list of dict
  - calculated_price: float or None


### 5. templates/insurance.html
- Page Title: Select Insurance Coverage
- Element IDs:
  - insurance-page (Div)
  - insurance-options (Div): container for insurance plans
  - select-insurance-{insurance_id} (Radio): select insurance plan
  - insurance-description (Div): shows selected insurance description
  - insurance-price (Div): shows selected insurance price
  - confirm-booking-button (Button)
- Navigation:
  - confirm-booking-button: submits insurance selection, possibly redirects
- Context Variables:
  - insurance_plans: list of dict
  - selected_insurance: dict or None


### 6. templates/rental_history.html
- Page Title: Rental History
- Element IDs:
  - history-page (Div)
  - rentals-table (Table): columns: ID, vehicle, dates, location, status
  - view-rental-details-{rental_id} (Button): view details of rental
  - status-filter (Dropdown)
  - back-to-dashboard (Button): url_for('dashboard')
- Navigation:
  - back-to-dashboard: url_for('dashboard')
- Context Variables:
  - rentals: list of dict
  - status_filter: str


### 7. templates/reservations.html
- Page Title: My Reservations
- Element IDs:
  - reservations-page (Div)
  - reservations-list (Div): list all reservations
  - modify-reservation-button-{reservation_id} (Button)
  - cancel-reservation-button-{reservation_id} (Button)
  - sort-by-date-button (Button)
  - back-to-dashboard (Button): url_for('dashboard')
- Navigation:
  - back-to-dashboard: url_for('dashboard')
- Context Variables:
  - reservations: list of dict


### 8. templates/special_requests.html
- Page Title: Special Requests
- Element IDs:
  - requests-page (Div)
  - select-reservation (Dropdown)
  - driver-assistance-checkbox (Checkbox)
  - gps-option-checkbox (Checkbox)
  - child-seat-quantity (Input)
  - special-notes (Textarea)
  - submit-requests-button (Button)
- Navigation:
  - submit-requests-button: submits form data
- Context Variables:
  - reservations: list of dict
  - form_data: dict or None


### 9. templates/locations.html
- Page Title: Pickup and Dropoff Locations
- Element IDs:
  - locations-page (Div)
  - locations-list (Div)
  - location-detail-button-{location_id} (Button)
  - hours-filter (Dropdown)
  - search-location-input (Input)
  - back-to-dashboard (Button): url_for('dashboard')
- Navigation:
  - back-to-dashboard: url_for('dashboard')
- Context Variables:
  - locations: list of dict
  - hours_filter: str
  - search_query: str


---

## Section 3: Data File Schemas

### vehicles.txt
- Stores: All vehicle details for renting, availability and pricing.
- Format (pipe-delimited):
  vehicle_id|make|model|vehicle_type|daily_rate|seats|transmission|fuel_type|status
- Fields:
  - vehicle_id: int
  - make: str
  - model: str
  - vehicle_type: str (Economy, Compact, Sedan, SUV, Luxury)
  - daily_rate: float
  - seats: int
  - transmission: str (Automatic, Manual)
  - fuel_type: str (Petrol, Diesel, Electric, Hybrid)
  - status: str (Available, Unavailable)
- Example lines:
  1|Toyota|Camry|Sedan|55.00|5|Automatic|Petrol|Available
  2|Honda|CR-V|SUV|75.00|7|Automatic|Petrol|Available
  3|BMW|X5|Luxury|150.00|5|Automatic|Diesel|Available


### customers.txt
- Stores: All customer personal and license info.
- Format:
  customer_id|name|email|phone|driver_license|license_expiry
- Fields:
  - customer_id: int
  - name: str
  - email: str
  - phone: str
  - driver_license: str
  - license_expiry: date (YYYY-MM-DD)
- Examples:
  1|Alice Johnson|alice@example.com|555-0101|D1234567|2026-06-15
  2|Bob Williams|bob@example.com|555-0102|D2345678|2027-03-20


### locations.txt
- Stores: Rental locations and availability
- Format:
  location_id|city|address|phone|hours|available_vehicles
- Fields:
  - location_id: int
  - city: str
  - address: str
  - phone: str
  - hours: str (24/7, 09:00-18:00, etc.)
  - available_vehicles: int
- Examples:
  1|New York|123 Main St, NYC|555-1000|24/7|12
  2|Los Angeles|456 Oak Ave, LA|555-2000|09:00-18:00|8


### rentals.txt
- Stores: Rental transactions with dates, locations, pricing, status
- Format:
  rental_id|vehicle_id|customer_id|pickup_date|dropoff_date|pickup_location|dropoff_location|total_price|status
- Fields:
  - rental_id: int
  - vehicle_id: int
  - customer_id: int
  - pickup_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)
  - dropoff_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)
  - pickup_location: str (city or specific location name)
  - dropoff_location: str
  - total_price: float
  - status: str (Completed, Active, Cancelled)
- Examples:
  1|1|1|2025-02-01|2025-02-05|New York|Los Angeles|275.00|Completed
  2|2|2|2025-02-10|2025-02-12|Los Angeles|New York|150.00|Active


### insurance.txt
- Stores: Insurance plan options for rentals
- Format:
  insurance_id|plan_name|description|daily_cost|coverage_limit|deductible
- Fields:
  - insurance_id: int
  - plan_name: str
  - description: str
  - daily_cost: float
  - coverage_limit: str|int (e.g., 50000 or "Unlimited")
  - deductible: int or float
- Examples:
  1|Basic Coverage|Liability only, min coverage|5.00|50000|1000
  2|Standard Coverage|Collision and theft protection|12.00|250000|500
  3|Premium Coverage|Full comprehensive protection|18.00|Unlimited|0


### reservations.txt
- Stores: Reservation details tied to rentals with insurance and special requests
- Format:
  reservation_id|rental_id|vehicle_id|customer_id|status|insurance_id|special_requests
- Fields:
  - reservation_id: int
  - rental_id: int
  - vehicle_id: int
  - customer_id: int
  - status: str (Confirmed, Active, Cancelled)
  - insurance_id: int
  - special_requests: str (free text)
- Examples:
  1|1|1|1|Confirmed|2|Driver assistance requested
  2|2|2|2|Active|1|GPS and child seat needed


---

END OF DESIGN SPECIFICATIONS

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <title>Search Vehicles</title>
</head>
<body>
    <div id="main-container">
        <h1>Search Vehicles</h1>
        <div id="search-page">
            <form method="get" action="{{ url_for('vehicle_search') }}">
                <label for="location-filter">Pickup Location:</label>
                <select id="location-filter" name="location">
                    <option value="">All</option>
                    {% for loc in locations %}
                    <option value="{{ loc.city }}" {% if filters.location == loc.city %}selected{% endif %}>{{ loc.city }}</option>
                    {% endfor %}
                </select>

                <label for="vehicle-type-filter">Vehicle Type:</label>
                <select id="vehicle-type-filter" name="vehicle_type">
                    <option value="">All</option>
                    {% for vt in vehicle_types %}
                    <option value="{{ vt }}" {% if filters.vehicle_type == vt %}selected{% endif %}>{{ vt }}</option>
                    {% endfor %}
                </select>

                <label for="date-range-input">Date Range:</label>
                <input type="text" id="date-range-input" name="date_range" value="{{ filters.date_range }}" placeholder="YYYY-MM-DD to YYYY-MM-DD" />

                <button type="submit">Filter</button>
            </form>

            <div id="vehicles-grid">
                {% for vehicle in vehicles %}

     | | /locations                | locations_page          | GET            | locations.html              | locations: list[dict], hours_filter: str, search_query: str                                     |  ### Route Details  - **/** (root_redirect): redirects to `/dashboard` to enforce dashboard as the start page. - **/dashboard**: Displays main dashboard with featured vehicles and promotions.    - featured_vehicles: List of vehicle dictionaries including vehicle_id, make, model, daily_rate, etc.   - promotions: List of promotion dictionaries, each containing title, description.  - **/search**: Displays search page with filters and all vehicles matching filters.    - vehicles: List of vehicle dictionaries with availability and details.   - locations: List of location search_query: str   ---  ## Section 3: Data File Schemas  ### vehicles.txt - Stores: All vehicle details for renting, availability and pricing. - Format (pipe-delimited):   vehicle_id|make|model|vehicle_type|daily_rate|seats|transmission|fuel_type|status - Fields:   - vehicle_id: int   - make: str   - model: str   - vehicle_type: str (Economy, Compact, Sedan, SUV, Luxury)   - daily_rate: float   - seats: int   - transmission: str (Automatic, Manual)   - fuel_type: str (Petrol, Diesel, Electric, Hybrid)   - status: str (Available, Unavailable) - Example lines:   1|Toyota|Camry|Sedan|55.00|5|Automatic|Petrol|Available   2|Honda|CR-V|SUV|75.00|7|Automatic|Petrol|Available   3|BMW|X5|Luxury|150.00|5|Automatic|Diesel|Available   ### customers.txt - Stores: All customer personal and license info. - Format:   customer_id|name|email|phone|driver_license|license_expiry - Fields:   - customer_id: int   - name: str   - email: str   - phone: str   - # CarRental Web Application Design Specifications

---

## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification (Backend)

| Route Path                 | Function Name           | HTTP Method(s) | Template File              | Context Variables                                                                                  |
|----------------------------|-------------------------|----------------|----------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| /                          | root_redirect           | GET            | N/A (redirect to /dashboard) | None                                                                                             |
| /dashboard                 | dashboard               | GET            | dashboard.html              | featured_vehicles: list[dict], promotions: list[dict]                                           |
| /search                   | vehicle_search          | GET            | search.html                 | vehicles: list[dict], locations: list[dict], vehicle_types: list[str], filters: dict[str,str]   |
| /vehicle/<int:vehicle_id> | vehicle_details         | GET            | vehicle_details.html        | vehicle: dict, reviews: list[dict]                                                              |
| /booking                  | booking                 | GET, POST      | booking.html                | pickup_locations: list[dict], dropoff_locations: list[dict], calculated_price: float or None     |
| /insurance                | insurance_options       | GET, POST      | insurance.html              | insurance_plans: list[dict], selected_insurance: dict or None                                   |
| /rental-history           | rental_history          | GET            | rental_history.html         | rentals: list[dict], status_filter: str                                                          |
| /reservations             | reservations_management | GET, POST      | reservations.html           | reservations: list[dict]                                                                         |
| /special-requests         | special_requests        | GET, POST      | special_requests.html       | reservations: list[dict], form_data: dict or None                                               |
| /locations                | locations_page          | GET            | locations.html              | locations: list[dict], hours_filter: str, search_query: str                                     |

### Route Details

- **/** (root_redirect): redirects to `/dashboard` to enforce dashboard as the start page.
- **/dashboard**: Displays main dashboard with featured vehicles and promotions.

  - featured_vehicles: List of vehicle dictionaries including vehicle_id, make, model, daily_rate, etc.
  - promotions: List of promotion dictionaries, each containing title, description.

- **/search**: Displays search page with filters and all vehicles matching filters.

  - vehicles: List of vehicle dictionaries with availability and details.
  - locations: List of location dictionaries for filtering.
  - vehicle_types: List[str] of vehicle type strings (`Economy`, `Compact`, `Sedan`, `SUV`, `Luxury`).
  - filters: Dict[str,str] current filter values for location, vehicle_type, date_range.

- **/vehicle/<int:vehicle_id>**: Shows detailed information about one vehicle.

  - vehicle: Dict with vehicle fields.
  - reviews: List of review dicts related to vehicle.

- **/booking**: Displays and processes booking form.

  - GET context: pickup_locations, dropoff_locations.
  - POST context: same + calculated_price (float) after price calculation.

- **/insurance**: Insurance options selection page.

  - insurance_plans: List of insurance dictionaries.
  - selected_insurance: Selected insurance dictionary or None.

- **/rental-history**: Displays rental history.

  - rentals: List of rental dictionaries.
  - status_filter: Current selected status filter (e.g., "All", "Active", etc.)

- **/reservations**: Manages reservations with possible actions POSTed.

  - reservations: List of reservation dictionaries.

- **/special-requests**: Add special requests to selected reservation.

  - reservations: List of current reservations.
  - form_data: Dict of submitted special requests or None.

- **/locations**: Displays locations with filters and search.

  - locations: List of location dictionaries.
  - hours_filter: Current hours filter value.
  - search_query: Current text search query string.


---

## Section 2: HTML Template Specifications (Frontend)

### 1. templates/dashboard.html
- Page Title: Car Rental Dashboard
- Element IDs:

  - search-vehicles-button (Button): Navigates to vehicle search page via url_for('vehicle_search').
  - my-reservations-button (Button): Navigates to reservations page via url_for('reservations_management').
  - promotions-section (Div): Displays current promotions and offers.
- Navigation:
  - search-vehicles-button: url_for('vehicle_search')
  - my-reservations-button: url_for('reservations_management')
- Context Variables:
  - featured_vehicles: list of dict with vehicle fields.
  - promotions: list of dict with promotion fields.

  - date-range-input (Input): Rental date range input

  - view-details-button-{vehicle_id} (Button): Each vehicle's details button with dynamic id, where {vehicle_id} is vehicle's ID

## Section 3: Data File Schemas

### vehicles.txt
- Stores: All vehicle details for renting, availability and pricing.
- Format (pipe-delimited):
  vehicle_id|make|model|vehicle_type|daily_rate|seats|transmission|fuel_type|status
- Fields:
  - vehicle_id: int
  - make: str
  - model: str
  - vehicle_type: str (Economy, Compact, Sedan, SUV, Luxury)
  - daily_rate: float
  - seats: int
  - transmission: str (Automatic, Manual)
  - fuel_type: str (Petrol, Diesel, Electric, Hybrid)
  - status: str (Available, Unavailable)
- Example lines:
  1|Toyota|Camry|Sedan|55.00|5|Automatic|Petrol|Available
  2|Honda|CR-V|SUV|75.00|7|Automatic|Petrol|Available
  3|BMW|X5|Luxury|150.00|5|Automatic|Diesel|Available


### customers.txt
- Stores: All customer personal and license info.
- Format:
  customer_id|name|email|phone|driver_license|license_expiry
- Fields:
  - customer_id: int
  - name: str
  - email: str
  - phone: str
  - driver_license: str
  - license_expiry: date (YYYY-MM-DD)
- Examples:
  1|Alice Johnson|alice@example.com|555-0101|D1234567|2026-06-15
  2|Bob Williams|bob@example.com|555-0102|D2345678|2027-03-20


### locations.txt
- Stores: Rental locations and availability
- Format:
  location_id|city|address|phone|hours|available_vehicles
- Fields:
  - location_id: int
  - city: str
  - address: str
  - phone: str
  - hours: str (24/7, 09:00-18:00, etc.)
  - available_vehicles: int
- Examples:
  1|New York|123 Main St, NYC|555-1000|24/7|12
  2|Los Angeles|456 Oak Ave, LA|555-2000|09:00-18:00|8


### rentals.txt
- Stores: Rental transactions with dates, locations, pricing, status
- Format:
  rental_id|vehicle_id|customer_id|pickup_date|dropoff_date|pickup_location|dropoff_location|total_price|status
- Fields:
  - rental_id: int
  - vehicle_id: int
  - customer_id: int
  - pickup_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)
  - dropoff_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)
  - pickup_location: str (city or specific location name)
  - dropoff_location: str
  - total_price: float
  - status: str (Completed, Active, Cancelled)
- Examples:
  1|1|1|2025-02-01|2025-02-05|New York|Los Angeles|275.00|Completed
  2|2|2|2025-02-10|2025-02-12|Los Angeles|New York|150.00|Active


### insurance.txt
- Stores: Insurance plan options for rentals
- Format:
  insurance_id|plan_name|description|daily_cost|coverage_limit|deductible
- Fields:
  - insurance_id: int
  - plan_name: str
  - description: str
  - daily_cost: float
  - coverage_limit: str|int (e.g., 50000 or "Unlimited")
  - deductible: int or float
- Examples:
  1|Basic Coverage|Liability only, min coverage|5.00|50000|1000
  2|Standard Coverage|Collision and theft protection|12.00|250000|500
  3|Premium Coverage|Full comprehensive protection|18.00|Unlimited|0


### reservations.txt
- Stores: Reservation details tied to rentals with insurance and special requests
- Format:
  reservation_id|rental_id|vehicle_id|customer_id|status|insurance_id|special_requests
- Fields:
  - reservation_id: int
  - rental_id: int
  - vehicle_id: int
  - customer_id: int
  - status: str (Confirmed, Active, Cancelled)
  - insurance_id: int
  - special_requests: str (free text)
- Examples:
  1|1|1|1|Confirmed|2|Driver assistance requested
  2|2|2|2|Active|1|GPS and child seat needed


---

END OF DESIGN SPECIFICATIONS


=== app.py ===
from flask import Flask, render_template, request, redirect, url_for
import csv
from datetime import datetime

app = Flask(__name__)

# Data loading and parsing with required fields and corrections

def load_vehicles():
    vehicles = []
    with open('vehicles.txt', 'r') as f:
        reader = csv.DictReader(f, delimiter='|', fieldnames=[
            'vehicle_id', 'make', 'model', 'vehicle_type', 'daily_rate', 'seats', 'transmission', 'fuel_type', 'status'
        ])
        for row in reader:
            try:
                vehicle = {
                    'vehicle_id': int(row['vehicle_id']),
                    'make': row['make'],
                    'model': row['model'],
                    'vehicle_type': row['vehicle_type'],
                    'daily_rate': float(row['daily_rate']),
                    'seats': int(row['seats']),
                    'transmission': row['transmission'],
                    'fuel_type': row['fuel_type'],
                    'status': row['status']
                }
                vehicles.append(vehicle)
            except Exception:
                continue
    return vehicles

def load_locations():
    locations = []
    with open('locations.txt', 'r') as f:
        reader = csv.DictReader(f, delimiter='|', fieldnames=[
            'location_id', 'city', 'address', 'phone', 'hours', 'available_vehicles'
        ])
        for row in reader:
            try:
                location = {
                    'location_id': int(row['location_id']),
                    'city': row['city'],
                    'address': row['address'],
                    'phone': row['phone'],
                    'hours': row['hours'],
                    'available_vehicles': row['available_vehicles'].split(',') if row['available_vehicles'] else []
                }
                locations.append(location)
            except Exception:
                continue
    return locations

def load_rentals():
    rentals = []
    with open('rentals.txt', 'r') as f:
        reader = csv.DictReader(f, delimiter='|', fieldnames=[
            'rental_id', 'vehicle_id', 'customer_id', 'pickup_date', 'dropoff_date', 'pickup_location', 'dropoff_location', 'total_price', 'status'
        ])
        for row in reader:
            try:
                rental = {
                    'rental_id': int(row['rental_id']),
                    'vehicle_id': int(row['vehicle_id']),
                    'customer_id': int(row['customer_id']),
                    'pickup_date': row['pickup_date'],
                    'dropoff_date': row['dropoff_date'],
                    'pickup_location': row['pickup_location'],
                    'dropoff_location': row['dropoff_location'],
                    'total_price': float(row['total_price']),
                    'status': row['status']
                }
                rentals.append(rental)
            except Exception:
                continue
    return rentals

def load_insurance():
    plans = []
    with open('insurance.txt', 'r') as f:
        reader = csv.DictReader(f, delimiter='|', fieldnames=[
            'insurance_id', 'plan_name', 'description', 'daily_cost', 'coverage_limit', 'deductible'
        ])
        for row in reader:
            try:
                plan = {
                    'insurance_id': int(row['insurance_id']),
                    'plan_name': row['plan_name'],
                    'description': row['description'],
                    'daily_cost': float(row['daily_cost']),
                    'coverage_limit': row['coverage_limit'],
                    'deductible': float(row['deductible'])
                }
                # coverage_limit can be "Unlimited" or numeric
                try:
                    plan['coverage_limit'] = float(plan['coverage_limit'])
                except ValueError:
                    # Keep it as string
                    pass
                plans.append(plan)
            except Exception:
                continue
    return plans

def load_reservations():
    reservations = []
    with open('reservations.txt', 'r') as f:
        reader = csv.DictReader(f, delimiter='|', fieldnames=[
            'reservation_id', 'rental_id', 'vehicle_id', 'customer_id', 'status', 'insurance_id', 'special_requests'
        ])
        for row in reader:
            try:
                reservation = {
                    'reservation_id': int(row['reservation_id']),
                    'rental_id': int(row['rental_id']),
                    'vehicle_id': int(row['vehicle_id']),
                    'customer_id': int(row['customer_id']),
                    'status': row['status'],
                    'insurance_id': int(row['insurance_id']) if row['insurance_id'] else None,
                    'special_requests': row['special_requests']
                }
                reservations.append(reservation)
            except Exception:
                continue
    return reservations

# Route: root redirect to /dashboard
@app.route('/')
def root_redirect():
    return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))

# Route: /dashboard
@app.route('/dashboard')
def dashboard():
    vehicles = load_vehicles()
    featured_vehicles = vehicles[:5]  # Example: first 5 vehicles featured
    promotions = [
        {'title': 'Winter Sale', 'description': 'Up to 20% off on SUVs'},
        {'title': 'Weekend Discount', 'description': '15% off for weekend rentals'}
    ]
    return render_template('dashboard.html', featured_vehicles=featured_vehicles, promotions=promotions)

# Route: /search - vehicle search
@app.route('/search')
def vehicle_search():
    vehicles = load_vehicles()
    locations = load_locations()
    vehicle_types = sorted(list(set(v['vehicle_type'] for v in vehicles)))

    # Fetch filter selections
    selected_location = request.args.get('location', '')
    selected_vehicle_type = request.args.get('vehicle_type', '')

    # Filter vehicles based on selected filters
    filtered_vehicles = vehicles
    if selected_location:
        # Filter vehicles available at selected_location
        filtered_vehicles = [v for v in filtered_vehicles if str(v['vehicle_id']) in sum((loc['available_vehicles'] for loc in locations if loc['city'].lower() == selected_location.lower()), [])]
    if selected_vehicle_type:
        filtered_vehicles = [v for v in filtered_vehicles if v['vehicle_type'] == selected_vehicle_type]

    # Context current filters
    current_filters = {
        'location': selected_location,
        'vehicle_type': selected_vehicle_type
    }

    return render_template('search.html', vehicles=filtered_vehicles, locations=locations, vehicle_types=vehicle_types, current_filters=current_filters)

# Route: /vehicle/<vehicle_id>
@app.route('/vehicle/<int:vehicle_id>')
def vehicle_details(vehicle_id):
    vehicles = load_vehicles()
    vehicle = next((v for v in vehicles if v['vehicle_id'] == vehicle_id), None)
    if not vehicle:
        return "Vehicle not found", 404
    reviews = []  # No reviews data, empty list
    return render_template('vehicle_details.html', vehicle=vehicle, reviews=reviews)

# Route: /booking - GET to show form, POST to calculate price
@app.route('/booking', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def booking():
    vehicles = load_vehicles()
    locations = load_locations()
    dropoff_locations = [loc['city'] for loc in locations]

    if request.method == 'POST':
        try:
            vehicle_id = int(request.form.get('vehicle_id'))
            pickup_location = request.form.get('pickup_location')
            dropoff_location = request.form.get('dropoff_location')
            pickup_date_str = request.form.get('pickup_date')
            dropoff_date_str = request.form.get('dropoff_date')

            vehicle = next((v for v in vehicles if v['vehicle_id'] == vehicle_id), None)
            if not vehicle:
                return "Invalid vehicle", 400

            pickup_date = datetime.strptime(pickup_date_str, '%Y-%m-%d')
            dropoff_date = datetime.strptime(dropoff_date_str, '%Y-%m-%d')

            rental_days = (dropoff_date - pickup_date).days + 1
            if rental_days <= 0:
                calculated_price = 0.0
            else:
                calculated_price = rental_days * vehicle['daily_rate']

            return render_template('booking.html', vehicles=vehicles,
                                   dropoff_locations=dropoff_locations,
                                   calculated_price=calculated_price,
                                   selected_vehicle=vehicle)
        except Exception:
            return "Invalid data", 400

    # GET method
    return render_template('booking.html', vehicles=vehicles, dropoff_locations=dropoff_locations, calculated_price=None, selected_vehicle=None)

# Route: /rental-history
@app.route('/rental-history')
def rental_history():
    rentals = load_rentals()
    status_filter = request.args.get('status', '')
    if status_filter:
        rentals = [r for r in rentals if r['status'].lower() == status_filter.lower()]
    return render_template('rental_history.html', rentals=rentals, status_filter=status_filter)

# Route: /locations GET
@app.route('/locations')
def locations_page():
    locations = load_locations()
    search_query = request.args.get('search_query', '').lower()
    if search_query:
        locations = [loc for loc in locations if search_query in loc['city'].lower() or search_query in loc['address'].lower()]
    return render_template('locations.html', locations=locations, search_query=search_query)

# CarRental Web Application Design Specifications

---

## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification (Backend)

| Route Path                 | Function Name           | HTTP Method(s) | Template File              | Context Variables                                                                                  |
|----------------------------|-------------------------|----------------|----------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| /                          | root_redirect           | GET            | N/A (redirect to /dashboard) | None                                                                                             |
| /dashboard                 | dashboard               | GET            | dashboard.html              | featured_vehicles: list[dict], promotions: list[dict]                                           |
| /search                   | vehicle_search          | GET            | search.html                 | vehicles: list[dict], locations: list[dict], vehicle_types: list[str], filters: dict[str,str]   |
| /vehicle/<int:vehicle_id> | vehicle_details         | GET            | vehicle_details.html        | vehicle: dict, reviews: list[dict]                                                              |
| /booking                  | booking                 | GET, POST      | booking.html                | pickup_locations: list[dict], dropoff_locations: list[dict], calculated_price: float or None     |
| /insurance                | insurance_options       | GET, POST      | insurance.html              | insurance_plans: list[dict], selected_insurance: dict or None                                   |
| /rental-history           | rental_history          | GET            | rental_history.html         | rentals: list[dict], status_filter: str                                                          |
| /reservations             | reservations_management | GET, POST      | reservations.html           | reservations: list[dict]                                                                         |
| /special-requests         | special_requests        | GET, POST      | special_requests.html       | reservations: list[dict], form_data: dict or None                                               |
| /locations                | locations_page          | GET            | locations.html              | locations: list[dict], hours_filter: str, search_query: str                                     |

### Route Details

- **/** (root_redirect): redirects to `/dashboard` to enforce dashboard as the start page.
- **/dashboard**: Displays main dashboard with featured vehicles and promotions.

  - featured_vehicles: List of vehicle dictionaries including vehicle_id, make, model, daily_rate, etc.
  - promotions: List of promotion dictionaries, each containing title, description.

- **/search**: Displays search page with filters and all vehicles matching filters.

  - vehicles: List of vehicle dictionaries with availability and details.
  - locations: List of location dictionaries for filtering.
  - vehicle_types: List[str] of vehicle type strings (`Economy`, `Compact`, `Sedan`, `SUV`, `Luxury`).
  - filters: Dict[str,str] current filter values for location, vehicle_type, date_range.

- **/vehicle/<int:vehicle_id>**: Shows detailed information about one vehicle.

  - vehicle: Dict with vehicle fields.
  - reviews: List of review dicts related to vehicle.

- **/booking**: Displays and processes booking form.

  - GET context: pickup_locations, dropoff_locations.
  - POST context: same + calculated_price (float) after price calculation.

- **/insurance**: Insurance options selection page.

  - insurance_plans: List of insurance dictionaries.
  - selected_insurance: Selected insurance dictionary or None.

- **/rental-history**: Displays rental history.

  - rentals: List of rental dictionaries.
  - status_filter: Current selected status filter (e.g., "All", "Active", etc.)

- **/reservations**: Manages reservations with possible actions POSTed.

  - reservations: List of reservation dictionaries.

- **/special-requests**: Add special requests to selected reservation.

  - reservations: List of current reservations.
  - form_data: Dict of submitted special requests or None.

- **/locations**: Displays locations with filters and search.

  - locations: List of location dictionaries.
  - hours_filter: Current hours filter value.
  - search_query: Current text search query string.


---

---

## Section 3: Data File Schemas

### vehicles.txt
- Stores: All vehicle details for renting, availability and pricing.
- Format (pipe-delimited):
  vehicle_id|make|model|vehicle_type|daily_rate|seats|transmission|fuel_type|status
- Fields:
  - vehicle_id: int
  - make: str
  - model: str
  - vehicle_type: str (Economy, Compact, Sedan, SUV, Luxury)
  - daily_rate: float
  - seats: int
  - transmission: str (Automatic, Manual)
  - fuel_type: str (Petrol, Diesel, Electric, Hybrid)
  - status: str (Available, Unavailable)
- Example lines:
  1|Toyota|Camry|Sedan|55.00|5|Automatic|Petrol|Available
  2|Honda|CR-V|SUV|75.00|7|Automatic|Petrol|Available
  3|BMW|X5|Luxury|150.00|5|Automatic|Diesel|Available


### customers.txt
- Stores: All customer personal and license info.
- Format:
  customer_id|name|email|phone|driver_license|license_expiry
- Fields:
  - customer_id: int
  - name: str
  - email: str
  - phone: str
  - driver_license: str
  - license_expiry: date (YYYY-MM-DD)
- Examples:
  1|Alice Johnson|alice@example.com|555-0101|D1234567|2026-06-15
  2|Bob Williams|bob@example.com|555-0102|D2345678|2027-03-20


### locations.txt
- Stores: Rental locations and availability
- Format:
  location_id|city|address|phone|hours|available_vehicles
- Fields:
  - location_id: int
  - city: str
  - address: str
  - phone: str
  - hours: str (24/7, 09:00-18:00, etc.)
  - available_vehicles: int
- Examples:
  1|New York|123 Main St, NYC|555-1000|24/7|12
  2|Los Angeles|456 Oak Ave, LA|555-2000|09:00-18:00|8


### rentals.txt
- Stores: Rental transactions with dates, locations, pricing, status
- Format:
  rental_id|vehicle_id|customer_id|pickup_date|dropoff_date|pickup_location|dropoff_location|total_price|status
- Fields:
  - rental_id: int
  - vehicle_id: int
  - customer_id: int
  - pickup_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)
  - dropoff_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)
  - pickup_location: str (city or specific location name)
  - dropoff_location: str
  - total_price: float
  - status: str (Completed, Active, Cancelled)
- Examples:
  1|1|1|2025-02-01|2025-02-05|New York|Los Angeles|275.00|Completed
  2|2|2|2025-02-10|2025-02-12|Los Angeles|New York|150.00|Active


### insurance.txt
- Stores: Insurance plan options for rentals
- Format:
  insurance_id|plan_name|description|daily_cost|coverage_limit|deductible
- Fields:
  - insurance_id: int
  - plan_name: str
  - description: str
  - daily_cost: float
  - coverage_limit: str|int (e.g., 50000 or "Unlimited")
  - deductible: int or float
- Examples:
  1|Basic Coverage|Liability only, min coverage|5.00|50000|1000
  2|Standard Coverage|Collision and theft protection|12.00|250000|500
  3|Premium Coverage|Full comprehensive protection|18.00|Unlimited|0


### reservations.txt
- Stores: Reservation details tied to rentals with insurance and special requests
- Format:
  reservation_id|rental_id|vehicle_id|customer_id|status|insurance_id|special_requests
- Fields:
  - reservation_id: int
  - rental_id: int
  - vehicle_id: int
  - customer_id: int
  - status: str (Confirmed, Active, Cancelled)
  - insurance_id: int
  - special_requests: str (free text)
- Examples:
  1|1|1|1|Confirmed|2|Driver assistance requested
  2|2|2|2|Active|1|GPS and child seat needed


---

4. Data loading functions often omit or misorder fields, e.g., load_locations misses several fields, load_rentals uses wrong field names (e.g., 'return_date' instead of 'dropoff_date'), load_insurance tries to convert 'coverage_limit' (which can be strings like 'Unlimited') to float causing errors.

5. POST methods for routes like /reservations and /special-requests are incomplete or missing.

Please strictly follow route names, HTTP methods, template file names, context variable names, and fully implement data loading/writing per design_spec.md. Validate fields carefully and handle all specified routes with correct function names.
